Fragment shader: ../p9/p9.frag
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |struct LightSource {
  4 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
  5 |  vec4 positionWorld;
  6 |  vec4 positionEye;
  7 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
  8 |  int directional;
  9 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 10 |  int enabled;
 11 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 12 |  vec3 attenuation;
 13 |};
 14 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 15 |  LightSource lights[4];
 16 |};
 17 |
 18 |layout (binding=0) uniform sampler2D colores;
 19 |layout (binding=8) uniform sampler2D normales;
 20 |layout (binding=4) uniform sampler2D brillos;
 21 |// Descomenta este sampler cuando est칠s preparado para usarlo
 22 |//layout (binding=12) uniform sampler2D alturas;
 23 |
 24 |uniform bool useParallax;
 25 |
 26 |in VS_OUT
 27 |{
 28 |    vec3 fPosition;
 29 |    vec2 texCoord;
 30 |    vec3 tangentLightPos;
 31 |    vec3 tangentViewPos;
 32 |    vec3 tangentFPos;
 33 |} fs_in;
 34 |
 35 |out vec4 fragColor;
 36 |
 37 |void main()
 38 |{
 39 |	// Este c칩digo accede a los uniforms para que el compilador no los
 40 |	// descarte y pueda arrancar el programa. 
 41 |	// NO HACE NADA QUE TE PUEDA SERVIR. Sustit칰yelo por tu c칩digo.
 42 |
 43 |	if (useParallax) {
 44 |		fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 45 |	} else {
 46 |		vec4 c = texture(colores, TexCoord);
 47 |		vec4 n = texture(normales, TexCoord);
 48 |		vec4 b = texture(brillos, TexCoord);
 49 |		if (lights[0].positionEye.y > 2.0) {
 50 |			fragColor = c * n * b;
 51 |		} else
 52 |			fragColor = c;
 53 |	}
 54 |}
 55 |

  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |struct LightSource {
 12 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
 13 |  vec4 positionWorld;
 14 |  vec4 positionEye;
 15 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
 16 |  int directional;
 17 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 18 |  int enabled;
 19 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 20 |  vec3 attenuation;
 21 |};
 22 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 23 |  LightSource lights[4];
 24 |};
 25 |
 26 |// Atributos del v本tice (sistema de coordenadas del modelo)
 27 |in vec4 position;
 28 |in vec2 texCoord;
 29 |in vec3 normal;
 30 |in vec3 tangent;
 31 |
 32 |// A人de las variables out que necesites
 33 |out VS_OUT
 34 |{
 35 |    vec3 fPosition;
 36 |    vec2 texCoord;
 37 |    vec3 tangentLightPos;
 38 |    vec3 tangentViewPos;
 39 |    vec3 tangentFPos;
 40 |} vs_out;
 41 |
 42 |void main()
 43 |{
 44 |	vs_out.texCoord = vec2(texCoord);
 45 |    vs_out.fPosition = vec3(modelMatrix*position);
 46 |	gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * position;
 47 |
 48 |    vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix * normal);
 49 |    vec3 T = normalize(mat3(modelMatrix) * tangent);
 50 |    vec3 B = normalize(mat3(modelMatrix) * cross(eN, tangent));
 51 |    vec3 N = normalize(mat3(modelMatrix) * eN);
 52 |    mat3 TBN = transpose(mat3(T, B, N));
 53 |
 54 |    vs_out.TangentLightPos = TBN * vec3(lights.positionWorld);
 55 |    //vs_out.TangentViewPos  = TBN * viewPos;
 56 |    vs_out.TangentFragPos  = TBN * vs_out.FragPos;
 57 |}

Fragment shader: ../p9/p9.frag
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |struct LightSource {
  4 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
  5 |  vec4 positionWorld;
  6 |  vec4 positionEye;
  7 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
  8 |  int directional;
  9 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 10 |  int enabled;
 11 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 12 |  vec3 attenuation;
 13 |};
 14 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 15 |  LightSource lights[4];
 16 |};
 17 |
 18 |layout (binding=0) uniform sampler2D colores;
 19 |layout (binding=8) uniform sampler2D normales;
 20 |layout (binding=4) uniform sampler2D brillos;
 21 |// Descomenta este sampler cuando est칠s preparado para usarlo
 22 |//layout (binding=12) uniform sampler2D alturas;
 23 |
 24 |uniform bool useParallax;
 25 |
 26 |in VS_OUT
 27 |{
 28 |    vec3 fPosition;
 29 |    vec2 texCoord;
 30 |    vec3 tangentLightPos;
 31 |    vec3 tangentViewPos;
 32 |    vec3 tangentFPos;
 33 |} fs_in;
 34 |
 35 |out vec4 fragColor;
 36 |
 37 |vec2 ParallaxMapping(vec2 texCoord, vec3 viewDir)
 38 |{ 
 39 |    float height =  texture(normales, texCoord).r;    
 40 |    vec2 p = viewDir.xy / viewDir.z * (height * height_scale);
 41 |    return texCoord - p;    
 42 |} 
 43 |
 44 |void main()
 45 |{
 46 |	if (useParallax)
 47 |	{
 48 |		fragColor = vec4(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
 49 |	}
 50 |	else
 51 |	{
 52 |		vec4 c = texture(colores, fs_in.texCoord);
 53 |		vec4 n = texture(normales, fs_in.texCoord);
 54 |		vec4 b = texture(brillos, fs_in.texCoord);
 55 |		if (lights[0].positionEye.y > 2.0)
 56 |		{
 57 |			fragColor = c * n * b;
 58 |		}
 59 |		else
 60 |			fragColor = c;
 61 |	}
 62 |}
 63 |

Fragment shader: ../p9/p9.frag
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |struct LightSource {
  4 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
  5 |  vec4 positionWorld;
  6 |  vec4 positionEye;
  7 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
  8 |  int directional;
  9 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 10 |  int enabled;
 11 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 12 |  vec3 attenuation;
 13 |};
 14 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 15 |  LightSource lights[4];
 16 |};
 17 |
 18 |layout (binding=0) uniform sampler2D colores;
 19 |layout (binding=8) uniform sampler2D normales;
 20 |layout (binding=4) uniform sampler2D brillos;
 21 |// Descomenta este sampler cuando est칠s preparado para usarlo
 22 |//layout (binding=12) uniform sampler2D alturas;
 23 |uniform float depth;
 24 |
 25 |uniform bool useParallax;
 26 |
 27 |in VS_OUT
 28 |{
 29 |    vec3 fPosition;
 30 |    vec2 texCoord;
 31 |    vec3 tangentLightPos;
 32 |    vec3 tangentViewPos;
 33 |    vec3 tangentFPos;
 34 |} fs_in;
 35 |
 36 |out vec4 fragColor;
 37 |
 38 |vec2 ParallaxMapping(vec2 texCoord, vec3 viewDir)
 39 |{ 
 40 |    float height =  texture(normales, texCoord).r;    
 41 |    vec2 p = viewDir.xy / viewDir.z * (height * depth);
 42 |    return texCoord - p;    
 43 |} 
 44 |
 45 |void main()
 46 |{
 47 |	if (useParallax)
 48 |	{
 49 |		vec3 viewDir   = normalize(fs_in.tangentViewPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
 50 |		vec2 texCoords = ParallaxMapping(fs_in.texCoord,  viewDir);
 51 |
 52 |		vec3 diffuse = texture(colores, texCoords);
 53 |		vec3 normal  = texture(normales, texCoords);
 54 |		normal = normalize(normal * 2.0 - 1.0);
 55 |
 56 |		vec3 halfwayDir = normalize(lightDir + viewDir);  
 57 |        spec = pow(max(dot(normal, halfwayDir), 0.0), 16.0);
 58 |	}
 59 |	else
 60 |	{
 61 |		vec4 c = texture(colores, fs_in.texCoord);
 62 |		vec4 n = texture(normales, fs_in.texCoord);
 63 |		vec4 b = texture(brillos, fs_in.texCoord);
 64 |		if (lights[0].positionEye.y > 2.0)
 65 |		{
 66 |			fragColor = c * n * b;
 67 |		}
 68 |		else
 69 |			fragColor = c;
 70 |	}
 71 |}
 72 |

Fragment shader: ../p9/p9.frag
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |struct LightSource {
  4 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
  5 |  vec4 positionWorld;
  6 |  vec4 positionEye;
  7 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
  8 |  int directional;
  9 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 10 |  int enabled;
 11 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 12 |  vec3 attenuation;
 13 |};
 14 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 15 |  LightSource lights[4];
 16 |};
 17 |
 18 |layout (binding=0) uniform sampler2D colores;
 19 |layout (binding=8) uniform sampler2D normales;
 20 |layout (binding=4) uniform sampler2D brillos;
 21 |// Descomenta este sampler cuando est칠s preparado para usarlo
 22 |//layout (binding=12) uniform sampler2D alturas;
 23 |uniform float depth;
 24 |
 25 |uniform bool useParallax;
 26 |
 27 |in VS_OUT
 28 |{
 29 |    vec3 fPosition;
 30 |    vec2 texCoord;
 31 |    vec3 tangentLightPos;
 32 |    vec3 tangentViewPos;
 33 |    vec3 tangentFPos;
 34 |} fs_in;
 35 |
 36 |out vec4 fragColor;
 37 |
 38 |vec2 ParallaxMapping(vec2 texCoord, vec3 viewDir)
 39 |{ 
 40 |    float height =  texture(normales, texCoord).r;    
 41 |    vec2 p = viewDir.xy / viewDir.z * (height * depth);
 42 |    return texCoord - p;    
 43 |} 
 44 |
 45 |void main()
 46 |{
 47 |	if (useParallax)
 48 |	{
 49 |		vec3 viewDir   = normalize(fs_in.tangentViewPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
 50 |		vec2 texCoords = ParallaxMapping(fs_in.texCoord,  viewDir);
 51 |
 52 |		vec3 diffuse = vec3(texture(colores, texCoords));
 53 |		vec3 normal  = vec3(texture(normales, texCoords));
 54 |		normal = normalize(normal * 2.0 - 1.0);
 55 |
 56 |		vec3 halfwayDir = normalize(lightDir + viewDir);  
 57 |        spec = pow(max(dot(normal, halfwayDir), 0.0), 16.0);
 58 |	}
 59 |	else
 60 |	{
 61 |		vec4 c = texture(colores, fs_in.texCoord);
 62 |		vec4 n = texture(normales, fs_in.texCoord);
 63 |		vec4 b = texture(brillos, fs_in.texCoord);
 64 |		if (lights[0].positionEye.y > 2.0)
 65 |		{
 66 |			fragColor = c * n * b;
 67 |		}
 68 |		else
 69 |			fragColor = c;
 70 |	}
 71 |}
 72 |

[Fri May 22 13:08:08 2020] ERR: [program.cpp (223)] Error compilando el shader:0(68) : error C1008: undefined variable "FragColor"

Fragment shader: ../p9/p9.frag
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |struct LightSource {
  4 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
  5 |  vec4 positionWorld;
  6 |  vec4 positionEye;
  7 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
  8 |  int directional;
  9 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 10 |  int enabled;
 11 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 12 |  vec3 attenuation;
 13 |};
 14 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 15 |  LightSource lights[4];
 16 |};
 17 |
 18 |layout (binding=0) uniform sampler2D colores;
 19 |layout (binding=8) uniform sampler2D normales;
 20 |layout (binding=4) uniform sampler2D brillos;
 21 |// Descomenta este sampler cuando est칠s preparado para usarlo
 22 |layout (binding=12) uniform sampler2D alturas;
 23 |uniform float depth;
 24 |
 25 |uniform bool useParallax;
 26 |
 27 |in VS_OUT
 28 |{
 29 |    vec3 fPosition;
 30 |    vec2 texCoord;
 31 |    vec3 tangentLightPos;
 32 |    vec3 tangentViewPos;
 33 |    vec3 tangentFPos;
 34 |} fs_in;
 35 |
 36 |out vec4 fragColor;
 37 |
 38 |vec2 ParallaxMapping(vec2 texCoord, vec3 viewDir)
 39 |{ 
 40 |    float height =  texture(alturas, texCoord).r;     
 41 |    return texCoord - viewDir.xy * (height * depth); 
 42 |} 
 43 |
 44 |void main()
 45 |{
 46 |	if (useParallax)
 47 |	{
 48 |		vec3 viewDir = normalize(fs_in.tangentViewPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
 49 |		vec2 texCoords = ParallaxMapping(fs_in.texCoord,  viewDir);       
 50 |		if(texCoords.x > 1.0 || texCoords.y > 1.0 || texCoords.x < 0.0 || texCoords.y < 0.0)
 51 |			discard;
 52 |
 53 |		vec3 normal = texture(normales, texCoords).rgb;
 54 |		normal = normalize(normal * 2.0 - 1.0);
 55 |
 56 |		vec3 c = texture(colores, fs_in.texCoord).xyz;
 57 |		vec3 ambient = 0.1 * c;
 58 |
 59 |		vec3 lightDir = normalize(fs_in.tangentLightPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
 60 |		float diff = max(dot(lightDir, normal), 0.0);
 61 |		vec3 diffuse = diff * c;
 62 |
 63 |		vec3 reflectDir = reflect(-lightDir, normal);
 64 |		vec3 halfwayDir = normalize(lightDir + viewDir);  
 65 |		float spec = pow(max(dot(normal, halfwayDir), 0.0), 32.0);
 66 |
 67 |		vec3 specular = vec3(0.2) * spec;
 68 |		FragColor = vec4(ambient + diffuse + specular, 1.0);
 69 |	}
 70 |	else
 71 |	{
 72 |		vec4 c = texture(colores, fs_in.texCoord);
 73 |		vec4 n = texture(normales, fs_in.texCoord);
 74 |		vec4 b = texture(brillos, fs_in.texCoord);
 75 |		if (lights[0].positionEye.y > 2.0)
 76 |		{
 77 |			fragColor = c * n * b;
 78 |		}
 79 |		else
 80 |			fragColor = c;
 81 |	}
 82 |}
 83 |

Fragment shader: ../p9/p9.frag
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |struct LightSource {
  4 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
  5 |  vec4 positionWorld;
  6 |  vec4 positionEye;
  7 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
  8 |  int directional;
  9 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 10 |  int enabled;
 11 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 12 |  vec3 attenuation;
 13 |};
 14 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 15 |  LightSource lights[4];
 16 |};
 17 |
 18 |layout (binding=0) uniform sampler2D colores;
 19 |layout (binding=8) uniform sampler2D normales;
 20 |layout (binding=4) uniform sampler2D brillos;
 21 |// Descomenta este sampler cuando est칠s preparado para usarlo
 22 |layout (binding=12) uniform sampler2D alturas;
 23 |uniform float depth;
 24 |
 25 |uniform bool useParallax;
 26 |
 27 |in VS_OUT
 28 |{
 29 |    vec3 fPosition;
 30 |    vec2 texCoord;
 31 |    vec3 tangentLightPos;
 32 |    vec3 tangentViewPos;
 33 |    vec3 tangentFPos;
 34 |} fs_in;
 35 |
 36 |out vec4 fragColor;
 37 |
 38 |vec2 ParallaxMapping(vec2 texCoord, vec3 viewDir)
 39 |{ 
 40 |    float height =  texture(alturas, texCoord).r;     
 41 |    return texCoord - viewDir.xy * (height * depth); 
 42 |} 
 43 |
 44 |void main()
 45 |{
 46 |	if (useParallax)
 47 |	{
 48 |		vec3 viewDir = normalize(fs_in.tangentViewPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
 49 |		vec2 texCoords = ParallaxMapping(fs_in.texCoord,  viewDir);       
 50 |		if(texCoords.x > 1.0 || texCoords.y > 1.0 || texCoords.x < 0.0 || texCoords.y < 0.0)
 51 |			discard;
 52 |
 53 |		vec3 normal = texture(normales, texCoords).rgb;
 54 |		normal = normalize(normal * 2.0 - 1.0);
 55 |
 56 |		vec3 c = texture(colores, fs_in.texCoord).xyz;
 57 |		vec3 ambient = 0.1 * c;
 58 |
 59 |		vec3 lightDir = normalize(fs_in.tangentLightPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
 60 |		float diff = max(dot(lightDir, normal), 0.0);
 61 |		vec3 diffuse = diff * c;
 62 |
 63 |		vec3 reflectDir = reflect(-lightDir, normal);
 64 |		vec3 halfwayDir = normalize(lightDir + viewDir);  
 65 |		float spec = pow(max(dot(normal, halfwayDir), 0.0), 32.0);
 66 |
 67 |		vec3 specular = vec3(0.2) * spec;
 68 |		fragColor = vec4(ambient + diffuse + specular, 1.0);
 69 |	}
 70 |	else
 71 |	{
 72 |		//vec4 c = texture(colores, fs_in.texCoord);
 73 |		//vec4 n = texture(normales, fs_in.texCoord);
 74 |		//vec4 b = texture(brillos, fs_in.texCoord);
 75 |
 76 |		vec3 normal = texture(normalMap, fs_in.texCoord).rgb;
 77 |		normal = normalize(normal * 2.0 - 1.0);  // this normal is in tangent space
 78 |   
 79 |		// get diffuse color
 80 |		vec3 c = texture(diffuseMap, fs_in.texCoord).rgb;
 81 |		// ambient
 82 |		vec3 ambient = 0.1 * c;
 83 |		// diffuse
 84 |		vec3 lightDir = normalize(fs_in.tangentLightPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
 85 |		float diff = max(dot(lightDir, normal), 0.0);
 86 |		vec3 diffuse = diff * c;
 87 |		// specular
 88 |		vec3 viewDir = normalize(fs_in.tangentViewPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
 89 |		vec3 reflectDir = reflect(-lightDir, normal);
 90 |		vec3 halfwayDir = normalize(lightDir + viewDir);  
 91 |		float spec = pow(max(dot(normal, halfwayDir), 0.0), 32.0);
 92 |
 93 |		vec3 specular = vec3(0.2) * spec;
 94 |		//fragColor = vec4(ambient + diffuse + specular, 1.0);
 95 |
 96 |		if (lights[0].positionEye.y > 2.0)
 97 |		{
 98 |			//fragColor = c * n * b;
 99 |			fragColor = vec4(ambient + diffuse + specular, 1.0);
100 |		}
101 |		else
102 |			//fragColor = c;
103 |			fragColor = vec4(diffuse, 1.0);
104 |	}
105 |}
106 |

Fragment shader: ../p9/p9.frag
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |struct LightSource {
  4 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
  5 |  vec4 positionWorld;
  6 |  vec4 positionEye;
  7 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
  8 |  int directional;
  9 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 10 |  int enabled;
 11 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 12 |  vec3 attenuation;
 13 |};
 14 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 15 |  LightSource lights[4];
 16 |};
 17 |
 18 |layout (binding=0) uniform sampler2D colores;
 19 |layout (binding=8) uniform sampler2D normales;
 20 |layout (binding=4) uniform sampler2D brillos;
 21 |// Descomenta este sampler cuando est칠s preparado para usarlo
 22 |layout (binding=12) uniform sampler2D alturas;
 23 |uniform float depth;
 24 |
 25 |uniform bool useParallax;
 26 |
 27 |in VS_OUT
 28 |{
 29 |    vec3 fPosition;
 30 |    vec2 texCoord;
 31 |    vec3 tangentLightPos;
 32 |    vec3 tangentViewPos;
 33 |    vec3 tangentFPos;
 34 |} fs_in;
 35 |
 36 |out vec4 fragColor;
 37 |
 38 |vec2 ParallaxMapping(vec2 texCoord, vec3 viewDir)
 39 |{ 
 40 |    float height =  texture(alturas, texCoord).r;     
 41 |    return texCoord - viewDir.xy * (height * depth); 
 42 |} 
 43 |
 44 |void main()
 45 |{
 46 |	if (useParallax)
 47 |	{
 48 |		vec3 viewDir = normalize(fs_in.tangentViewPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
 49 |		vec2 texCoords = ParallaxMapping(fs_in.texCoord,  viewDir);       
 50 |		if(texCoords.x > 1.0 || texCoords.y > 1.0 || texCoords.x < 0.0 || texCoords.y < 0.0)
 51 |			discard;
 52 |
 53 |		vec3 normal = texture(normales, texCoords).rgb;
 54 |		normal = normalize(normal * 2.0 - 1.0);
 55 |
 56 |		vec3 c = texture(colores, fs_in.texCoord).xyz;
 57 |		vec3 ambient = 0.1 * c;
 58 |
 59 |		vec3 lightDir = normalize(fs_in.tangentLightPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
 60 |		float diff = max(dot(lightDir, normal), 0.0);
 61 |		vec3 diffuse = diff * c;
 62 |
 63 |		vec3 reflectDir = reflect(-lightDir, normal);
 64 |		vec3 halfwayDir = normalize(lightDir + viewDir);  
 65 |		float spec = pow(max(dot(normal, halfwayDir), 0.0), 32.0);
 66 |
 67 |		vec3 specular = texture(brillos, fs_in.texCoord).rgb * spec;
 68 |		fragColor = vec4(ambient + diffuse + specular, 1.0);
 69 |	}
 70 |	else
 71 |	{
 72 |		//vec4 c = texture(colores, fs_in.texCoord);
 73 |		//vec4 n = texture(normales, fs_in.texCoord);
 74 |		//vec4 b = texture(brillos, fs_in.texCoord);
 75 |
 76 |		vec3 normal = texture(normales, fs_in.texCoord).rgb;
 77 |		normal = normalize(normal * 2.0 - 1.0);  // this normal is in tangent space
 78 |   
 79 |		// get diffuse color
 80 |		vec3 c = texture(colores, fs_in.texCoord).rgb;
 81 |		// ambient
 82 |		vec3 ambient = 0.1 * c;
 83 |		// diffuse
 84 |		vec3 lightDir = normalize(fs_in.tangentLightPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
 85 |		float diff = max(dot(lightDir, normal), 0.0);
 86 |		vec3 diffuse = diff * c;
 87 |		// specular
 88 |		vec3 viewDir = normalize(fs_in.tangentViewPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
 89 |		vec3 reflectDir = reflect(-lightDir, normal);
 90 |		vec3 halfwayDir = normalize(lightDir + viewDir);  
 91 |		float spec = pow(max(dot(normal, halfwayDir), 0.0), 32.0);
 92 |
 93 |		vec3 specular = texture(brillos, texCoords).rgb * spec;
 94 |		//fragColor = vec4(ambient + diffuse + specular, 1.0);
 95 |
 96 |		if (lights[0].positionEye.y > 2.0)
 97 |		{
 98 |			//fragColor = c * n * b;
 99 |			fragColor = vec4(ambient + diffuse + specular, 1.0);
100 |		}
101 |		else
102 |			//fragColor = c;
103 |			fragColor = vec4(diffuse, 1.0);
104 |	}
105 |}
106 |

 12 |  vec3 attenuation;
 13 |};
 14 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 15 |  LightSource lights[4];
 16 |};
 17 |
 18 |layout (binding=0) uniform sampler2D colores;
 19 |layout (binding=8) uniform sampler2D normales;
 20 |layout (binding=4) uniform sampler2D brillos;
 21 |// Descomenta este sampler cuando est칠s preparado para usarlo
 22 |layout (binding=12) uniform sampler2D alturas;
 23 |uniform float depth;
 24 |
 25 |uniform bool useParallax;
 26 |
 27 |in VS_OUT
 28 |{
 29 |    vec3 fPosition;
 30 |    vec2 texCoord;
 31 |    vec3 tangentLightPos;
 32 |    vec3 tangentViewPos;
 33 |    vec3 tangentFPos;
 34 |} fs_in;
 35 |
 36 |out vec4 fragColor;
 37 |
 38 |vec2 ParallaxMapping(vec2 texCoord, vec3 viewDir)
 39 |{ 
 40 |    float height =  texture(alturas, texCoord).r;     
 41 |    return texCoord - viewDir.xy * (height * depth); 
 42 |}
 43 |vec2 ParallaxMapping3(vec2 texCoords, vec3 viewDir)
 44 |{ 
 45 |    // number of depth layers
 46 |    const float minLayers = 8;
 47 |    const float maxLayers = 32;
 48 |    float numLayers = mix(maxLayers, minLayers, abs(dot(vec3(0.0, 0.0, 1.0), viewDir)));  
 49 |    // calculate the size of each layer
 50 |    float layerDepth = 1.0 / numLayers;
 51 |    // depth of current layer
 52 |    float currentLayerDepth = 0.0;
 53 |    // the amount to shift the texture coordinates per layer (from vector P)
 54 |    vec2 P = viewDir.xy / viewDir.z * heightScale; 
 55 |    vec2 deltaTexCoords = P / numLayers;
 56 |  
 57 |    // get initial values
 58 |    vec2  currentTexCoords     = texCoords;
 59 |    float currentDepthMapValue = texture(depthMap, currentTexCoords).r;
 60 |      
 61 |    while(currentLayerDepth < currentDepthMapValue)
 62 |    {
 63 |        // shift texture coordinates along direction of P
 64 |        currentTexCoords -= deltaTexCoords;
 65 |        // get depthmap value at current texture coordinates
 66 |        currentDepthMapValue = texture(depthMap, currentTexCoords).r;  
 67 |        // get depth of next layer
 68 |        currentLayerDepth += layerDepth;  
 69 |    }
 70 |    
 71 |    // get texture coordinates before collision (reverse operations)
 72 |    vec2 prevTexCoords = currentTexCoords + deltaTexCoords;
 73 |
 74 |    // get depth after and before collision for linear interpolation
 75 |    float afterDepth  = currentDepthMapValue - currentLayerDepth;
 76 |    float beforeDepth = texture(depthMap, prevTexCoords).r - currentLayerDepth + layerDepth;
 77 | 
 78 |    // interpolation of texture coordinates
 79 |    float weight = afterDepth / (afterDepth - beforeDepth);
 80 |    vec2 finalTexCoords = prevTexCoords * weight + currentTexCoords * (1.0 - weight);
 81 |
 82 |    return finalTexCoords;
 83 |}
 84 |
 85 |void main()
 86 |{
 87 |	if (useParallax)
 88 |	{
 89 |		vec3 viewDir = normalize(fs_in.tangentViewPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
 90 |		vec2 texCoords = ParallaxMapping3(fs_in.texCoord,  viewDir);       
 91 |		if(texCoords.x > 1.0 || texCoords.y > 1.0 || texCoords.x < 0.0 || texCoords.y < 0.0)
 92 |			discard;
 93 |
 94 |		vec3 normal = texture(normales, texCoords).rgb;
 95 |		normal = normalize(normal * 2.0 - 1.0);
 96 |
 97 |		vec3 c = texture(colores, texCoords).xyz;
 98 |		vec3 ambient = 0.1 * c;
 99 |
100 |		vec3 lightDir = normalize(fs_in.tangentLightPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
101 |		float diff = max(dot(lightDir, normal), 0.0);
102 |		vec3 diffuse = diff * c;
103 |
104 |		vec3 reflectDir = reflect(-lightDir, normal);
105 |		vec3 halfwayDir = normalize(lightDir + viewDir);  
106 |		float spec = pow(max(dot(normal, halfwayDir), 0.0), 32.0);
107 |
108 |		vec3 specular = texture(brillos, texCoords).rgb * spec;
109 |		fragColor = vec4(ambient + diffuse + specular, 1.0);
110 |	}
111 |	else
112 |	{
113 |		//vec4 c = texture(colores, fs_in.texCoord);
114 |		//vec4 n = texture(normales, fs_in.texCoord);
115 |		//vec4 b = texture(brillos, fs_in.texCoord);
116 |
117 |		vec3 normal = texture(normales, fs_in.texCoord).rgb;
118 |		normal = normalize(normal * 2.0 - 1.0);  // this normal is in tangent space
119 |   
120 |		// get diffuse color
121 |		vec3 c = texture(colores, fs_in.texCoord).rgb;
122 |		// ambient
123 |		vec3 ambient = 0.1 * c;
124 |		// diffuse
125 |		vec3 lightDir = normalize(fs_in.tangentLightPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
126 |		float diff = max(dot(lightDir, normal), 0.0);
127 |		vec3 diffuse = diff * c;
128 |		// specular
129 |		vec3 viewDir = normalize(fs_in.tangentViewPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
130 |		vec3 reflectDir = reflect(-lightDir, normal);
131 |		vec3 halfwayDir = normalize(lightDir + viewDir);  
132 |		float spec = pow(max(dot(normal, halfwayDir), 0.0), 32.0);
133 |
134 |		vec3 specular = texture(brillos, fs_in.texCoord).rgb * spec;
135 |		//fragColor = vec4(ambient + diffuse + specular, 1.0);
136 |
137 |		if (lights[0].positionEye.y > 2.0)
138 |		{
139 |			//fragColor = c * n * b;
140 |			fragColor = vec4(ambient + diffuse + specular, 1.0);
141 |		}
142 |		else
143 |			//fragColor = c;
144 |			fragColor = vec4(diffuse, 1.0);
145 |	}
146 |}

132 |		float spec = pow(max(dot(normal, halfwayDir), 0.0), 32.0);
133 |
134 |		vec3 specular = texture(brillos, fs_in.texCoord).rgb * spec;
135 |		//fragColor = vec4(ambient + diffuse + specular, 1.0);
136 |
137 |		if (lights[0].positionEye.y > 2.0)
138 |		{
139 |			//fragColor = c * n * b;
140 |			fragColor = vec4(ambient + diffuse + specular, 1.0);
141 |		}
142 |		else
143 |			//fragColor = c;
144 |			fragColor = vec4(diffuse, 1.0);
145 |	}
146 |}

Fragment shader: ../p9/p9.frag
------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |struct LightSource {
  4 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
  5 |  vec4 positionWorld;
  6 |  vec4 positionEye;
  7 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
  8 |  int directional;
  9 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 10 |  int enabled;
 11 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 12 |  vec3 attenuation;
 13 |};
 14 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 15 |  LightSource lights[4];
 16 |};
 17 |
 18 |layout (binding=0) uniform sampler2D colores;
 19 |layout (binding=8) uniform sampler2D normales;
 20 |layout (binding=4) uniform sampler2D brillos;
 21 |// Descomenta este sampler cuando est칠s preparado para usarlo
 22 |layout (binding=12) uniform sampler2D alturas;
 23 |uniform float depth;
 24 |
 25 |uniform bool useParallax;
 26 |
 27 |in VS_OUT
 28 |{
 29 |    vec3 fPosition;
 30 |    vec2 texCoord;
 31 |    vec3 tangentLightPos;
 32 |    vec3 tangentViewPos;
 33 |    vec3 tangentFPos;
 34 |} fs_in;
 35 |
 36 |out vec4 fragColor;
 37 |
 38 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V)
 39 |{
 40 |  vec4 color = vec4(vec3(0.0f),1.0f);
 41 |  float shininess = 1;
 42 |  vec4 ambient = texture(colores, TexCoord);
 43 |  vec4 diffuse = ambient;
 44 |  //vec4 n = texture(normales, TexCoord);
 45 |  vec4 specular = texture(brillos, TexCoord);
 46 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++)
 47 |  {
 48 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 49 |      continue;
 50 |    vec3 L = normalize(pL[i]);
 51 |    int directCheck = lights[i].directional;
 52 |    float d = distance (L, pos);
 53 |    float aten = 1;
 54 |    if (directCheck==0)
 55 |    {
 56 |        aten = 1 / max ( 1, lights[i].attenuation[0] + lights[i].attenuation[1] * d + lights[i].attenuation[2] * pow(d,2) );
 57 |    }
 58 |    vec3 L_nagative = L*(-1.0f);
 59 |    float foco = 1.0;
 60 |    if (lights[i].directional==0 && lights[i].spotCutoff < 180.0)
 61 |    {
 62 |        float maxCosAngle = max(dot(L_nagative, lights[i].spotDirectionEye), 0.0);
 63 |        foco = maxCosAngle >= lights[i].spotCosCutoff ? foco = pow(maxCosAngle,lights[i].spotExponent) : 0.0;
 64 |    }
 65 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 66 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 67 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 68 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 69 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 70 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 71 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 72 |    }
 73 |
 74 |    color += aten * foco * (lights[i].ambient * ambient +
 75 |             lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
 76 |             lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult);
 77 |  }
 78 |  return color;
 79 |}
 80 |
 81 |vec2 ParallaxMapping(vec2 texCoord, vec3 viewDir)
 82 |{ 
 83 |    float height =  texture(alturas, texCoord).r;     
 84 |    return texCoord - viewDir.xy * (height * depth); 
 85 |}
 86 |vec2 ParallaxMapping2(vec2 texCoords, vec3 viewDir)
 87 |{ 
 88 |    // number of depth layers
 89 |    const float minLayers = 8;
 90 |    const float maxLayers = 32;
 91 |    float numLayers = mix(maxLayers, minLayers, abs(dot(vec3(0.0, 0.0, 1.0), viewDir)));  
 92 |    // calculate the size of each layer
 93 |    float layerDepth = 1.0 / numLayers;
 94 |    // depth of current layer
 95 |    float currentLayerDepth = 0.0;
 96 |    // the amount to shift the texture coordinates per layer (from vector P)
 97 |    vec2 P = viewDir.xy / viewDir.z * depth; 
 98 |    vec2 deltaTexCoords = P / numLayers;
 99 |  
100 |    // get initial values
101 |    vec2  currentTexCoords     = texCoords;
102 |    float currentDepthMapValue = texture(alturas, currentTexCoords).r;
103 |      
104 |    while(currentLayerDepth < currentDepthMapValue)
105 |    {
106 |        // shift texture coordinates along direction of P
107 |        currentTexCoords -= deltaTexCoords;
108 |        // get depthmap value at current texture coordinates
109 |        currentDepthMapValue = texture(alturas, currentTexCoords).r;  
110 |        // get depth of next layer
111 |        currentLayerDepth += layerDepth;  
112 |    }
113 |    
114 |    return currentTexCoords;
115 |}
116 |vec2 ParallaxMapping3(vec2 texCoords, vec3 viewDir)
117 |{ 
118 |    // number of depth layers
119 |    const float minLayers = 8;
120 |    const float maxLayers = 32;
121 |    float numLayers = mix(maxLayers, minLayers, abs(dot(vec3(0.0, 0.0, 1.0), viewDir)));  
122 |    // calculate the size of each layer
123 |    float layerDepth = 1.0 / numLayers;
124 |    // depth of current layer
125 |    float currentLayerDepth = 0.0;
126 |    // the amount to shift the texture coordinates per layer (from vector P)
127 |    vec2 P = viewDir.xy / viewDir.z * depth; 
128 |    vec2 deltaTexCoords = P / numLayers;
129 |  
130 |    // get initial values
131 |    vec2  currentTexCoords     = texCoords;
132 |    float currentDepthMapValue = texture(alturas, currentTexCoords).r;
133 |      
134 |    while(currentLayerDepth < currentDepthMapValue)
135 |    {
136 |        // shift texture coordinates along direction of P
137 |        currentTexCoords -= deltaTexCoords;
138 |        // get depthmap value at current texture coordinates
139 |        currentDepthMapValue = texture(alturas, currentTexCoords).r;  
140 |        // get depth of next layer
141 |        currentLayerDepth += layerDepth;  
142 |    }
143 |    
144 |    // get texture coordinates before collision (reverse operations)
145 |    vec2 prevTexCoords = currentTexCoords + deltaTexCoords;
146 |
147 |    // get depth after and before collision for linear interpolation
148 |    float afterDepth  = currentDepthMapValue - currentLayerDepth;
149 |    float beforeDepth = texture(alturas, prevTexCoords).r - currentLayerDepth + layerDepth;
150 | 
151 |    // interpolation of texture coordinates
152 |    float weight = afterDepth / (afterDepth - beforeDepth);
153 |    vec2 finalTexCoords = prevTexCoords * weight + currentTexCoords * (1.0 - weight);
154 |
155 |    return finalTexCoords;
156 |}
157 |
158 |void main()
159 |{
160 |	if (useParallax)
161 |	{
162 |		vec3 viewDir = normalize(fs_in.tangentViewPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
163 |		vec2 texCoords = ParallaxMapping2(fs_in.texCoord,  viewDir);       
164 |		if(texCoords.x > 1.0 || texCoords.y > 1.0 || texCoords.x < 0.0 || texCoords.y < 0.0)
165 |			discard;
166 |
167 |		vec3 normal = texture(normales, texCoords).rgb;
168 |		normal = normalize(normal * 2.0 - 1.0);
169 |
170 |		vec3 c = texture(colores, texCoords).xyz;
171 |		vec3 ambient = 0.1 * c;
172 |
173 |		vec3 lightDir = normalize(fs_in.tangentLightPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
174 |		float diff = max(dot(lightDir, normal), 0.0);
175 |		vec3 diffuse = diff * c;
176 |
177 |		vec3 reflectDir = reflect(-lightDir, normal);
178 |		vec3 halfwayDir = normalize(lightDir + viewDir);  
179 |		float spec = pow(max(dot(normal, halfwayDir), 0.0), 32.0);
180 |
181 |		vec3 specular = texture(brillos, texCoords).rgb * spec;
182 |		fragColor = vec4(ambient + diffuse + specular, 1.0);
183 |	}
184 |	else
185 |	{
186 |		//vec4 c = texture(colores, fs_in.texCoord);
187 |		//vec4 n = texture(normales, fs_in.texCoord);
188 |		//vec4 b = texture(brillos, fs_in.texCoord);
189 |
190 |		vec3 normal = texture(normales, fs_in.texCoord).rgb;
191 |		normal = normalize(normal * 2.0 - 1.0);  // this normal is in tangent space
192 |   
193 |		// get diffuse color
194 |		vec3 c = texture(colores, fs_in.texCoord).rgb;
195 |		// ambient
196 |		vec3 ambient = 0.1 * c;
197 |		// diffuse
198 |		vec3 lightDir = normalize(fs_in.tangentLightPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
199 |		float diff = max(dot(lightDir, normal), 0.0);
200 |		vec3 diffuse = diff * c;
201 |		// specular
202 |		vec3 viewDir = normalize(fs_in.tangentViewPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
203 |		vec3 reflectDir = reflect(-lightDir, normal);
204 |		vec3 halfwayDir = normalize(lightDir + viewDir);  
205 |		float spec = pow(max(dot(normal, halfwayDir), 0.0), 32.0);
206 |
207 |		vec3 specular = texture(brillos, fs_in.texCoord).rgb * spec;
208 |		//fragColor = vec4(ambient + diffuse + specular, 1.0);
209 |
210 |		if (lights[0].positionEye.y > 2.0)
211 |		{
212 |			//fragColor = c * n * b;
213 |			fragColor = vec4(ambient + diffuse + specular, 1.0);
214 |		}
215 |		else
216 |			//fragColor = c;
217 |			fragColor = vec4(diffuse, 1.0);
218 |	}
219 |}

 44 |  //vec4 n = texture(normales, TexCoord);
 45 |  vec4 specular = texture(brillos, TexCoord);
 46 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++)
 47 |  {
 48 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 49 |      continue;
 50 |    vec3 L = normalize(pL[i]);
 51 |    int directCheck = lights[i].directional;
 52 |    float d = distance (L, pos);
 53 |    float aten = 1;
 54 |    if (directCheck==0)
 55 |    {
 56 |        aten = 1 / max ( 1, lights[i].attenuation[0] + lights[i].attenuation[1] * d + lights[i].attenuation[2] * pow(d,2) );
 57 |    }
 58 |    vec3 L_nagative = L*(-1.0f);
 59 |    float foco = 1.0;
 60 |    if (lights[i].directional==0 && lights[i].spotCutoff < 180.0)
 61 |    {
 62 |        float maxCosAngle = max(dot(L_nagative, lights[i].spotDirectionEye), 0.0);
 63 |        foco = maxCosAngle >= lights[i].spotCosCutoff ? foco = pow(maxCosAngle,lights[i].spotExponent) : 0.0;
 64 |    }
 65 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 66 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 67 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 68 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 69 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 70 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 71 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 72 |    }
 73 |
 74 |    color += aten * foco * (lights[i].ambient * ambient +
 75 |             lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
 76 |             lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult);
 77 |  }
 78 |  return color;
 79 |}
 80 |
 81 |vec2 ParallaxMapping(vec2 texCoord, vec3 viewDir)
 82 |{ 
 83 |    float height =  texture(alturas, texCoord).r;     
 84 |    return texCoord - viewDir.xy * (height * depth); 
 85 |}
 86 |vec2 ParallaxMapping2(vec2 texCoords, vec3 viewDir)
 87 |{ 
 88 |    // number of depth layers
 89 |    const float minLayers = 8;
 90 |    const float maxLayers = 32;
 91 |    float numLayers = mix(maxLayers, minLayers, abs(dot(vec3(0.0, 0.0, 1.0), viewDir)));  
 92 |    // calculate the size of each layer
 93 |    float layerDepth = 1.0 / numLayers;
 94 |    // depth of current layer
 95 |    float currentLayerDepth = 0.0;
 96 |    // the amount to shift the texture coordinates per layer (from vector P)
 97 |    vec2 P = viewDir.xy / viewDir.z * depth; 
 98 |    vec2 deltaTexCoords = P / numLayers;
 99 |  
100 |    // get initial values
101 |    vec2  currentTexCoords     = texCoords;
102 |    float currentDepthMapValue = texture(alturas, currentTexCoords).r;
103 |      
104 |    while(currentLayerDepth < currentDepthMapValue)
105 |    {
106 |        // shift texture coordinates along direction of P
107 |        currentTexCoords -= deltaTexCoords;
108 |        // get depthmap value at current texture coordinates
109 |        currentDepthMapValue = texture(alturas, currentTexCoords).r;  
110 |        // get depth of next layer
111 |        currentLayerDepth += layerDepth;  
112 |    }
113 |    
114 |    return currentTexCoords;
115 |}
116 |vec2 ParallaxMapping3(vec2 texCoords, vec3 viewDir)
117 |{ 
118 |    // number of depth layers
119 |    const float minLayers = 8;
120 |    const float maxLayers = 32;
121 |    float numLayers = mix(maxLayers, minLayers, abs(dot(vec3(0.0, 0.0, 1.0), viewDir)));  
122 |    // calculate the size of each layer
123 |    float layerDepth = 1.0 / numLayers;
124 |    // depth of current layer
125 |    float currentLayerDepth = 0.0;
126 |    // the amount to shift the texture coordinates per layer (from vector P)
127 |    vec2 P = viewDir.xy / viewDir.z * depth; 
128 |    vec2 deltaTexCoords = P / numLayers;
129 |  
130 |    // get initial values
131 |    vec2  currentTexCoords     = texCoords;
132 |    float currentDepthMapValue = texture(alturas, currentTexCoords).r;
133 |      
134 |    while(currentLayerDepth < currentDepthMapValue)
135 |    {
136 |        // shift texture coordinates along direction of P
137 |        currentTexCoords -= deltaTexCoords;
138 |        // get depthmap value at current texture coordinates
139 |        currentDepthMapValue = texture(alturas, currentTexCoords).r;  
140 |        // get depth of next layer
141 |        currentLayerDepth += layerDepth;  
142 |    }
143 |    
144 |    // get texture coordinates before collision (reverse operations)
145 |    vec2 prevTexCoords = currentTexCoords + deltaTexCoords;
146 |
147 |    // get depth after and before collision for linear interpolation
148 |    float afterDepth  = currentDepthMapValue - currentLayerDepth;
149 |    float beforeDepth = texture(alturas, prevTexCoords).r - currentLayerDepth + layerDepth;
150 | 
151 |    // interpolation of texture coordinates
152 |    float weight = afterDepth / (afterDepth - beforeDepth);
153 |    vec2 finalTexCoords = prevTexCoords * weight + currentTexCoords * (1.0 - weight);
154 |
155 |    return finalTexCoords;
156 |}
157 |
158 |void main()
159 |{
160 |	if (useParallax)
161 |	{
162 |		vec3 viewDir = normalize(fs_in.tangentViewPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
163 |		vec2 texCoords = ParallaxMapping2(fs_in.texCoord,  viewDir);       
164 |		if(texCoords.x > 1.0 || texCoords.y > 1.0 || texCoords.x < 0.0 || texCoords.y < 0.0)
165 |			discard;
166 |
167 |		vec3 normal = texture(normales, texCoords).rgb;
168 |		normal = normalize(normal * 2.0 - 1.0);
169 |
170 |		vec3 c = texture(colores, texCoords).xyz;
171 |		vec3 ambient = 0.1 * c;
172 |
173 |		vec3 lightDir = normalize(fs_in.tangentLightPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
174 |		float diff = max(dot(lightDir, normal), 0.0);
175 |		vec3 diffuse = diff * c;
176 |
177 |		vec3 reflectDir = reflect(-lightDir, normal);
178 |		vec3 halfwayDir = normalize(lightDir + viewDir);  
179 |		float spec = pow(max(dot(normal, halfwayDir), 0.0), 32.0);
180 |
181 |		vec3 specular = texture(brillos, texCoords).rgb * spec;
182 |		fragColor = vec4(ambient + diffuse + specular, 1.0);
183 |	}
184 |	else
185 |	{
186 |		//vec4 c = texture(colores, fs_in.texCoord);
187 |		//vec4 n = texture(normales, fs_in.texCoord);
188 |		//vec4 b = texture(brillos, fs_in.texCoord);
189 |
190 |		vec3 normal = texture(normales, fs_in.texCoord).rgb;
191 |		normal = normalize(normal * 2.0 - 1.0);  // this normal is in tangent space
192 |   
193 |		// get diffuse color
194 |		vec3 c = texture(colores, fs_in.texCoord).rgb;
195 |		// ambient
196 |		vec3 ambient = 0.1 * c;
197 |		// diffuse
198 |		vec3 lightDir = normalize(fs_in.tangentLightPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
199 |		float diff = max(dot(lightDir, normal), 0.0);
200 |		vec3 diffuse = diff * c;
201 |		// specular
202 |		vec3 viewDir = normalize(fs_in.tangentViewPos - fs_in.tangentFPos);
203 |		vec3 reflectDir = reflect(-lightDir, normal);
204 |		vec3 halfwayDir = normalize(lightDir + viewDir);  
205 |		float spec = pow(max(dot(normal, halfwayDir), 0.0), 32.0);
206 |
207 |		vec3 specular = texture(brillos, fs_in.texCoord).rgb * spec;
208 |		//fragColor = vec4(ambient + diffuse + specular, 1.0);
209 |
210 |		if (lights[0].positionEye.y > 2.0)
211 |		{
212 |			//fragColor = c * n * b;
213 |			fragColor = vec4(ambient + diffuse + specular, 1.0);
214 |		}
215 |		else
216 |			//fragColor = c;
217 |			fragColor = vec4(diffuse, 1.0);
218 |	}
219 |}
220 |
